     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <h1 class="page-header">Office of the Chief Financial Officer</h1> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <ul class="nav nav-tabs sub-nav tab4"> 
        <li class="active"><a class="" href="index.html">Overview</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="staff/index.html">Staff</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="mission-goals/index.html">Mission &amp; Goals</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="strategic-investment/index.html">Strategic Investment</a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- Example row of columns --> 
     <div class="row-fluid"> 
      <div class="span4 hero-unit"> 
       <p>We manage and oversee systemwide financial management.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4">
       <p>The CFO division is responsible for the systemwide management and oversight of all aspects of financial management at the campuses, academic medical centers and Lawrence Berkeley National Laboratory. Responsibilities include oversight on accounting and financial controls, risk management, strategic sourcing, tax compliance, payroll coordination and long range financial planning. We are also responsible for external relationships with rating agencies, investment houses, banks, financial auditors and financial regulators.</p>
      </div> 
      <div class="span4"> 
       <div class="row-fluid dotted-bottom"> 
        <div class="span4 dept-head"> 
         <img alt="Peter J. Taylor" src="_images/shot_12_ptaylor_004 2.jpg" />
        </div> 
        <div class="span8"> 
         <p class="blue"> Peter J. Taylor </p> 
         <p>Executive Vice President, Chief Financial Officer</p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row-fluid"> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon staff" href="staff/index.html">Staff Directory</a>
        </div> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon org" href="_files/cfo_org_chart.pdf">Org Chart</a>
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row-fluid blustripe dept-unit"> 
      <h2 class="nobtm">DEPARTMENTS</h2> 
      <div class="row-fluid col5"> 
       <div class="span2"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/capital-markets-finance/index.html">Capital Markets Finance</a> </h3> 
        <p>Supports capital-raising activities systemwide.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/bondholder-information/index.html">Bondholder information</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/capital-markets-finance/resources/index.html">Resources</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/capital-markets-finance/resources/cmf-newsletter/index.html">CMF newsletter</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span2"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/financial-accounting/index.html">Financial Accounting</a> </h3> 
        <p>Provides systemwide financial management, reporting, policy and procedures.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/business-resource-center/index.html">Business Resource Center</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/financial-accounting/units/index.html">Staff and units</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/financial-accounting/policies-and-guidance/index.html">Policies and guidance</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/financial-accounting/financial-reports/index.html">Financial reports</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span2"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/financial-services-controls/index.html">Financial Services and Controls</a> </h3> 
        <p>Provides systemwide banking services and policy used in the administration of all UC funds.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/banking-treasury-services/index.html">Banking and Treasury Services</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/central-travel-management/index.html">Central Travel Management</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/loan-programs/index.html">Office of Loan Programs</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span2"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/procurement-services/index.html">Procurement Services</a> </h3> 
        <p>Develops and implements systemwide purchasing policies and strategies.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/procurement-services/supplier-information/index.html">Supplier information</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/procurement-services/policies-forms/index.html">Policies and forms</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/procurement-services/agreements-database/index.html">Agreements database</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span2"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/risk-services/index.html">Risk Services</a> </h3> 
        <p>Enables university faculty, staff and students to identify and manage risk.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/risk-services/loss-prevention-control/index.html">Loss prevention and control</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/enterprise-risk-management/index.html">Enterprise Risk Management (ERM)</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/risk-services/reports-resources/index.html">Reports and resources</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/risk-services/crisis-management/ucop-staff-emergency-procedures/index.html">Crisis management</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row less3 novrflw"> 
      <div class="span4 grybx"> 
       <h4>Working Smarter</h4> 
       <p><span><img align="left" alt="Brain" height="56" src="/_common/files/img/brain.png" style="margin: 0px 10px 0px 0px;" width="80" />Faced with diminishing state support, the UC community is working to&nbsp;<span>build a sustainable financial model to carry the university forward</span>.</span></p> 
       <p><span><span><a href="http://workingsmarter.universityofcalifornia.edu/">Learn more</a></span></span></p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4 grybx"> 
       <h4>UC Path</h4> 
       <p><img align="left" alt="students on stairs at UC Riverside" height="67" src="/_common/_images/UC_Riverside-016.jpg" style="margin: 6px 10px 0px 0px;" vspace="0" width="100" />UCPath will deploy a single payroll system and a single human resource system that meets the core needs of each campus and medical center while capturing the efficiencies, improved data and cost-savings of unified systems.</p> 
       <p><a href="http://ucpath.universityofcalifornia.edu/">Learn more</a></p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4 grybx"> 
       <h4>Enterprise Risk Management</h4> 
       <p><a href="/enterprise-risk-management/index.html"><img align="left" alt="ERM Logo" height="71" src="/risk-services/_images/erm_logo_gold_smaller.png" style="margin: 0px 15px 0px 0px;" vspace="0" width="80" /></a>UCOP's ERM program helps the university achieve its goals by strategically managing risks inherent to higher educational institutions.</p> 
       <p><a href="/enterprise-risk-management/index.html">Read more</a></p> 
      </div> 
     </div>

      var SCROLLBAR_WIDTH = 21;
      var CONTENT_PADDING = 50;
      var GUIDE_WIDTH = 230;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_2 = 1056;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_3 = 1262;
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;

      var spaceForContent = screenWidth - SCROLLBAR_WIDTH - CONTENT_PADDING;

      } else {

    };
    ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS = 'guide-pinned';
    ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS = 'show-guide';
    ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle = function() {
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;
      return screenWidth >= 1251;
    };
    (function() {
      var htmlEl = document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0];
      var classList = [htmlEl.className];
        if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle()) {
          classList.push(ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS);
            classList.push(ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS);
        }
        classList.push(' ', ytpreload.getSnapClass(
            true));
      htmlEl.className = classList.join(' ');
    })();
  </script>

              <h2 class="branded-page-module-title"> <a href="/playlist?list=PLbpi6ZahtOH4v_AzenOKhbQdvlMhZ3GU9" class="yt-uix-sessionlink branded-page-module-title-link spf-nolink" data-sessionlink="ei=o5MfU5SyIYOt-APn3YG4Cw"> <span class="branded-page-module-title-text"> <span class="">Women Who've Conquered 'Bossy'</span> </span> </a> <a href="/watch?v=6dynbzMlCcw&amp;list=PLbpi6ZahtOH4v_AzenOKhbQdvlMhZ3GU9" class="yt-uix-button  shelves-play yt-uix-sessionlink yt-uix-button-default yt-uix-button-size-small" data-sessionlink="ei=o5MfU5SyIYOt-APn3YG4Cw"><span class="yt-uix-button-icon-wrapper"><img class="yt-uix-button-icon yt-uix-button-icon-play-all" src="http://s.ytimg.com/yts/img/pixel-vfl3z5WfW.gif" alt="" title="" /></span><span class="yt-uix-button-content">Play </span></a> </h2>

              <h2 class="branded-page-module-title"> <a href="/playlist?list=PLbpi6ZahtOH7O7nYRJeRB9frtIHoedmxj" class="yt-uix-sessionlink branded-page-module-title-link spf-nolink" data-sessionlink="ei=o5MfU5SyIYOt-APn3YG4Cw"> <span class="branded-page-module-title-text"> <span class="">E-Waste: What You Can Do About It</span> </span> </a> <a href="/watch?v=qoDcOqewX5c&amp;list=PLbpi6ZahtOH7O7nYRJeRB9frtIHoedmxj" class="yt-uix-button  shelves-play yt-uix-sessionlink yt-uix-button-default yt-uix-button-size-small" data-sessionlink="ei=o5MfU5SyIYOt-APn3YG4Cw"><span class="yt-uix-button-icon-wrapper"><img class="yt-uix-button-icon yt-uix-button-icon-play-all" src="http://s.ytimg.com/yts/img/pixel-vfl3z5WfW.gif" alt="" title="" /></span><span class="yt-uix-button-content">Play </span></a> </h2> 
              <div class="shelf-description yt-ui-ellipsis yt-ui-ellipsis-2">

              <h2 class="branded-page-module-title"> <a href="/playlist?list=PLbpi6ZahtOH6Kzv1FbSOeN8Z5Qi_UVcj1" class="yt-uix-sessionlink branded-page-module-title-link spf-nolink" data-sessionlink="ei=o5MfU5SyIYOt-APn3YG4Cw"> <span class="branded-page-module-title-text"> <span class="">Daylight Savings: 10 Things To Do With That Extra Hour of Daylight</span> </span> </a> <a href="/watch?v=V0DQWyb2Wig&amp;list=PLbpi6ZahtOH6Kzv1FbSOeN8Z5Qi_UVcj1" class="yt-uix-button  shelves-play yt-uix-sessionlink yt-uix-button-default yt-uix-button-size-small" data-sessionlink="ei=o5MfU5SyIYOt-APn3YG4Cw"><span class="yt-uix-button-icon-wrapper"><img class="yt-uix-button-icon yt-uix-button-icon-play-all" src="http://s.ytimg.com/yts/img/pixel-vfl3z5WfW.gif" alt="" title="" /></span><span class="yt-uix-button-content">Play </span></a> </h2> 
              <div class="shelf-description yt-ui-ellipsis yt-ui-ellipsis-2">
                While you might not exactly spring forward after losing an hour of sleep, you gain an hour of sunlight. Enjoy your added daily dose of Vitamin D with these epic suggestions for Daylight Saving Time. 
              </div>

              <h2 class="branded-page-module-title"> <a href="/playlist?list=PLbpi6ZahtOH66bQaDvlwLVz0UED1e27ml" class="yt-uix-sessionlink branded-page-module-title-link spf-nolink" data-sessionlink="ei=o5MfU5SyIYOt-APn3YG4Cw"> <span class="branded-page-module-title-text"> <span class="">Daylight Savings Time: Explained</span> </span> </a> <a href="/watch?v=84aWtseb2-4&amp;list=PLbpi6ZahtOH66bQaDvlwLVz0UED1e27ml" class="yt-uix-button  shelves-play yt-uix-sessionlink yt-uix-button-default yt-uix-button-size-small" data-sessionlink="ei=o5MfU5SyIYOt-APn3YG4Cw"><span class="yt-uix-button-icon-wrapper"><img class="yt-uix-button-icon yt-uix-button-icon-play-all" src="http://s.ytimg.com/yts/img/pixel-vfl3z5WfW.gif" alt="" title="" /></span><span class="yt-uix-button-content">Play </span></a> </h2> 
              <div class="shelf-description yt-ui-ellipsis yt-ui-ellipsis-2">
                How does Daylight Savings Time work around the world? Who thought it up? And ... what is ?time? anyway? These theorists and scientists spent some time attempting to answer these questions and more.

        $(function () {
            $("#txtGoogleSearch").each(function () {

            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").focus(function () {
                $(this).removeClass("GoogleWatermark"); // handle all focus hints
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").blur(function () {
                ToggleHint(this); // handle all blur hints
            });
        });

        function ToggleHint(obj) {
            if ($(obj).val() == '') { $(obj).addClass("GoogleWatermark"); };

     <div class="span-18 last"> 
      <h3>Print and Submit Forms</h3> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-8 append-1"> 
      <p>You can now submit some of our forms directly online. Others can be printed and returned to the Highlander One Stop Shop (HOSS) on the first floor of the <a href="http://campusmap.ucr.edu/imap/index.html?loc=SSB">Student Services Building</a> or mailed to: </p> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-9 last"> 
      <strong>University of California, Riverside<br /> Office of the Registrar<br /> 2249 Student Services Building<br /> Riverside, CA 92521-0118</strong> 
     </div>

       <p class="footer_info"> <img src="/Images/saBldImage_registrar.jpg" width="120" height="87" alt="Student Serves Building" />The Office of the Registrar delivers accurate, prompt, courteous and consistent services to all students and constituents of UC Riverside. The Registrar takes a leadership role in management of registration, student academic records, course and classroom scheduling, classroom utilization, publications production, and data distribution. </p>

  <div class="pagewrapper"> 
   <h3 class="accessibility">Footer</h3> 
   <div id="colophon">
     The University of California, Riverside (
    <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/">www.ucr.edu</a>) is a doctoral research university, a living laboratory for groundbreaking exploration of issues critical to Inland Southern California, the state and communities around the world. Reflecting California's diverse culture, UCR's enrollment has exceeded 21,000 students. The campus opened a medical school in 2013 and has reached the heart of the Coachella Valley by way of the UCR Palm Desert Center. The campus has an annual statewide economic impact of more than $1 billion. A broadcast studio with fiber cable to the AT&amp;T Hollywood hub is available for live or taped interviews. UCR also has ISDN for radio interviews. To learn more, call (951) UCR-NEWS. 
   </div>
